# Test source

```ts
  1  | import { test, expect } from "@playwright/test";
  2  | 
  3  | const searchData = [
  4  |     { keyword: "playwright", expectedTitle: "playwright" },
  5  |     { keyword: "selenium", expectedTitle: "selenium" },
  6  |     { keyword: "cucumber", expectedTitle: "cucumber" },
  7  | ];
  8  | 
  9  | test.describe("Google search test", () => {
  10 |     for (const sd of searchData) {
  11 |         test(`search Flow - ${sd.keyword}`, async ({ page }) => {
  12 | 
  13 |             await page.goto("https://www.google.com/");
  14 |             await page.locator("textarea[name='q']").fill(sd.keyword);
  15 |             await page.locator("input[name='btnK']").first().click();
> 16 |             const fr = page.locator("h3").first();
     |                                                        ^ Error: locator.click: Test timeout of 60000ms exceeded.
  17 |             await fr.click();
  18 |             await expect(page).toHaveTitle(new RegExp(sd.expectedTitle, "i"));
  19 |         });
  20 |     }
  21 | });
```
